FROM [Roasters] AS [r]

SELECT [r].[Id], [r].[ContactEmail], [r].[ContactNumber], [r].[Description], [r].[InstagramProfileLink], [r].[Name], [r].[OfficeAddressId], [r].[Picture], [r].[TelegramProfileLink], [r].[VkProfileLink], [r].[WebSiteLink], [a].[Id], [a].[AddressStr], [a].[OpeningHours], [a].[RoasterId], [t0].[RoasterId], [t0].[TagId], [t0].[Id], [t0].[TagTitle]
FROM [Roasters] AS [r]
LEFT JOIN [Addresses] AS [a] ON [r].[OfficeAddressId] = [a].[Id]

FROM (
    SELECT TOP(1) [r].[Id], [r].[ContactEmail], [r].[ContactNumber], [r].[Description], [r].[InstagramProfileLink], [r].[Name], [r].[OfficeAddressId], [r].[Picture], [r].[TelegramProfileLink], [r].[VkProfileLink], [r].[WebSiteLink], [a].[Id] AS [Id0], [a].[AddressStr], [a].[OpeningHours], [a].[RoasterId]

    WHERE [r].[Name] = @__roasterName_0
) AS [t]

) AS [t1] ON [t].[Id] = [t1].[RoasterId]
